---
about_this_resource_text: '<p><strong>Description: </strong>How a certain spacetime
  duplicates the kinematics of Newtonian gravity for slow motion (continuation of
  lecture 9).  Spacetime curvature, deduced by examining parallel transport of a vector
  around an infinitesimal parallelogram, described by the Riemann tensor (a 4 index
  tensor with 20 independent components).</p> <p><strong>Instructor:</strong> Prof.
  Scott Hughes</p>'
course_id: 8-962-general-relativity-spring-2020

  <span m="4440280">that</span> <span m="4440360">additional</span> <span m="4440640">structure</span>
  <span m="4441060">is</span> <span m="4441180">essentially</span> <span m="4441510">filling</span>
  <span m="4441930">up</span> <span m="4442050">part</span> <span m="4442410">of</span>
  <span m="4442500">the</span> <span m="4442560">local</span> <span m="4442860">Lorentz</span>
  <span m="4443250">frame</span> <span m="4443520">around</span> <span m="4444360">the</span>
  <span m="4444480">center</span> <span m="4444780">of</span> <span m="4444900">mass</span>
  <span m="4445260">of</span> <span m="4445340">that</span> <span m="4445500">point,</span>
  <span m="4446820">and</span> <span m="4448650">they</span> <span m="4449340">couple</span>
  <span m="4449790">the</span> <span m="4449850">spacetime</span> <span m="4450330">and</span>
  <span m="4450420">push</span> <span m="4450610">it</span> <span m="4450660">away</span>
  <span m="4450840">from</span> <span m="4450990">the</span> <span m="4451050">geodesic.</span>
  <span m="4452220">This</span> <span m="4452370">Riemann</span> <span m="4452760">tensor</span>
  <span m="4453150">actually</span> <span m="4453390">describes</span> <span m="4454050">the</span>
  <span m="4454140">way</span> <span m="4454380">in</span> <span m="4454530">which</span>
  <span m="4454740">that</span> <span m="4454920">body</span> <span m="4455220">couples</span>
  <span m="4455910">to the</span> <span m="4456210">background</span> <span m="4456630">spacetime,</span>
  <span m="4457200">that</span> <span m="4457610">it</span> <span m="4457740">might</span>
  <span m="4457920">be</span> <span m="4458040">falling</span> <span m="4458460">in.</span>
  <span m="4459360">So</span> <span m="4459540">this</span> <span m="4459750">ends</span>
  <span m="4459930">up</span> <span m="4460020">playing</span> <span m="4460290">a</span>
  <span m="4460350">really</span> <span m="4460560">important</span> <span m="4460920">role.</span></p><p><span

  <span m="4472350">quantity</span> <span m="4472860">that</span> <span m="4472980">mathematically</span>

  <span m="4476370">there.</span></p><p><span m="4477790">So</span> <span m="4479280">I'm</span>
